# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

Use `sg_list_repos` to discover available repositories before searching.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

---

## Summary of Findings

I've identified all the Go source files that implement client-side retry and timeout policy in etcd:

### **Files (11 total)**
1. **client/v3/retry_interceptor.go** - gRPC unary and stream retry interceptors
2. **client/v3/retry.go** - Retry policy definitions and retry client wrappers
3. **client/v3/client.go** - Main client with dial balancer, health check, and auto-sync
4. **client/v3/kv.go** - KV interface for Put, Get, Delete, Txn operations
5. **client/v3/watch.go** - Watch streaming interface
6. **client/v3/lease.go** - Lease interface with keep-alive support
7. **client/v3/config.go** - Configuration with timeout and retry settings
8. **client/v3/internal/resolver/resolver.go** - Manual endpoint resolver
9. **client/v3/internal/endpoint/endpoint.go** - Endpoint interpretation and credentials management
10. **client/v3/naming/resolver/resolver.go** - gRPC resolver builder
11. **client/v3/naming/endpoints/endpoints.go** - Dynamic endpoint manager

### **Key Implementation Components**
- **Retry interceptors**: `unaryClientInterceptor()` and `streamClientInterceptor()` with exponential backoff and jitter
- **Retry policies**: `isSafeRetryImmutableRPC()` and `isSafeRetryMutableRPC()` protecting read/write semantics
- **Endpoint management**: `dialWithBalancer()` for load-balanced connection, `autoSync()` for periodic updates
- **Health checking**: `waitForConnection()` using gRPC health check service
- **Operation wrappers**: `retryKVClient`, `retryWatchClient`, `retryLeaseClient` for type-specific retry logic

policies through multiple interconnected components:\\n\\n## gRPC Retry Interceptors\\n\\n**client/v3/retry_interceptor.go** contains the core retry logic:\\n- `unaryClientInterceptor()`: Handles retry for unary RPC calls (Put, Get, Delete, Txn operations) with configurable max retries and exponential backoff\\n- `streamClientInterceptor()`: Handles retry for streaming RPC calls (Watch operations) with disabled retries by default for safety\\n- `waitRetryBackoff()`: Implements backoff logic between retry attempts with jitter to prevent thundering herd\\n\\n## Retry Policy and Error Handling\\n\\n**client/v3/retry.go** defines the retry semantics:\\n- `isSafeRetryImmutableRPC()`: Determines if immutable requests (Read operations) can be safely retried. Returns true only for Unavailable errors, otherwise stops retry to prevent duplicate reads\\n- `isSafeRetryMutableRPC()`: Determines if mutable requests (Write operations) can be safely retried. Only retries on Unavailable when initial connection failed, never on established connections to preserve write-at-most-once semantics\\n- `retryKVClient`: Wraps KV client with retry logic for Put, Range, Delete, Txn operations\\n- `retryWatchClient`: Wraps Watch client with retry logic for Watch streams\\n- `retryLeaseClient`: Wraps Lease client with retry logic for Grant, Revoke, KeepAlive operations\\n\\n## Endpoint Balancer and Health Check\\n\\n**client/v3/client.go** implements the endpoint management and health checking:\\n- `dialWithBalancer()`: Dials the client's current load-balanced resolver group using gRPC's built-in round-robin balancer\\n- `autoSync()`: Periodic endpoint synchronization (when AutoSyncInterval > 0) that fetches fresh cluster member information from the server\\n- `waitForConnection()`: Waits for gRPC connection to be ready using the health check service, with fallback for servers not exposing health endpoints\\n- `dialSetupOpts()`: Configures gRPC dial options including:\\n  - keepalive parameters (Time, Timeout, PermitWithoutStream)\\n  - transport credentials (TLS)\\n  - unary/stream interceptors with retry and backoff settings\\n\\n## Configuration and Timeout Settings\\n\\n**client/v3/config.go** defines timeout and retry configuration:\\n- `DialTimeout`: Timeout for initial connection establishment\\n- `DialKeepAliveTime`: Interval for client-side keepalive pings to detect broken connections\\n- `DialKeepAliveTimeout`: Timeout waiting for keepalive response before closing connection\\n- `MaxUnaryRetries`: Maximum retry attempts for unary calls (default: 3)\\n- `BackoffWaitBetween`: Base wait duration between retries\\n- `BackoffJitterFraction`: Jitter fraction to randomize backoff timing\\n\\n## KV, Watch, and Lease Operation Implementations\\n\\n**client/v3/kv.go**: Defines KV interface with Put, Get, Delete, Txn operations that use the wrapped retryKVClient\\n\\n**client/v3/watch.go**: Implements Watch interface for server push notifications, handles stream resumption on connection failures with closeSendErrTimeout (250ms)\\n\\n**client/v3/lease.go**: Implements Lease interface with Grant, Revoke, KeepAlive operations and keepAliveTimeout parameter for KeepAlive stream management. The `sendKeepAliveLoop()` sends periodic keep-alive requests to maintain lease liveliness.\\n\\n## Endpoint Resolution and Management\\n\\n**client/v3/internal/resolver/resolver.go**: Implements EtcdManualResolver using gRPC's manual.Builder for endpoint state management and updates\\n\\n**client/v3/naming/resolver/resolver.go**: Provides gRPC resolver builder using etcd's endpoint manager for dynamic endpoint discovery\\n\\n**client/v3/internal/endpoint/endpoint.go**: Interprets endpoint URLs (http, https, unix, unixs) and manages credentials requirements (CredsRequire, CredsDrop, CredsOptional)\\n\\n**client/v3/naming/endpoints/endpoints.go**: Manager interface for dynamically adding/deleting/listing endpoints backed by etcd storage\\n\\n## Overall Request Flow\\n\\n1. Client initialization calls `dialWithBalancer()` which uses the resolver to discover endpoints\\n2. `waitForConnection()` ensures the connection is healthy via gRPC health checks\\n3. `autoSync()` periodically refreshes endpoints in background\\n4. Unary calls go through `unaryClientInterceptor()` which applies retry logic with backoff\\n5. Stream calls (Watch) go through `streamClientInterceptor()` with retries disabled by default\\n6. `isSafeRetryImmutableRPC()` and `isSafeRetryMutableRPC()` guard retry decisions based on error type\\n7. KV operations use `retryKVClient`, Watch uses `retryWatchClient`, Lease uses `retryLeaseClient`\\n8. gRPC keepalive parameters ensure timely detection of broken connections\\n9. Lease keep-alive loop maintains lease TTL with `sendKeepAliveLoop()`\"\n}\n",

policies through multiple interconnected components:\\n\\n## gRPC Retry Interceptors\\n\\n**client/v3/retry_interceptor.go** contains the core retry logic:\\n- `unaryClientInterceptor()`: Handles retry for unary RPC calls (Put, Get, Delete, Txn operations) with configurable max retries and exponential backoff\\n- `streamClientInterceptor()`: Handles retry for streaming RPC calls (Watch operations) with disabled retries by default for safety\\n- `waitRetryBackoff()`: Implements backoff logic between retry attempts with jitter to prevent thundering herd\\n\\n## Retry Policy and Error Handling\\n\\n**client/v3/retry.go** defines the retry semantics:\\n- `isSafeRetryImmutableRPC()`: Determines if immutable requests (Read operations) can be safely retried. Returns true only for Unavailable errors, otherwise stops retry to prevent duplicate reads\\n- `isSafeRetryMutableRPC()`: Determines if mutable requests (Write operations) can be safely retried. Only retries on Unavailable when initial connection failed, never on established connections to preserve write-at-most-once semantics\\n- `retryKVClient`: Wraps KV client with retry logic for Put, Range, Delete, Txn operations\\n- `retryWatchClient`: Wraps Watch client with retry logic for Watch streams\\n- `retryLeaseClient`: Wraps Lease client with retry logic for Grant, Revoke, KeepAlive operations\\n\\n## Endpoint Balancer and Health Check\\n\\n**client/v3/client.go** implements the endpoint management and health checking:\\n- `dialWithBalancer()`: Dials the client's current load-balanced resolver group using gRPC's built-in round-robin balancer\\n- `autoSync()`: Periodic endpoint synchronization (when AutoSyncInterval > 0) that fetches fresh cluster member information from the server\\n- `waitForConnection()`: Waits for gRPC connection to be ready using the health check service, with fallback for servers not exposing health endpoints\\n- `dialSetupOpts()`: Configures gRPC dial options including:\\n  - keepalive parameters (Time, Timeout, PermitWithoutStream)\\n  - transport credentials (TLS)\\n  - unary/stream interceptors with retry and backoff settings\\n\\n## Configuration and Timeout Settings\\n\\n**client/v3/config.go** defines timeout and retry configuration:\\n- `DialTimeout`: Timeout for initial connection establishment\\n- `DialKeepAliveTime`: Interval for client-side keepalive pings to detect broken connections\\n- `DialKeepAliveTimeout`: Timeout waiting for keepalive response before closing connection\\n- `MaxUnaryRetries`: Maximum retry attempts for unary calls (default: 3)\\n- `BackoffWaitBetween`: Base wait duration between retries\\n- `BackoffJitterFraction`: Jitter fraction to randomize backoff timing\\n\\n## KV, Watch, and Lease Operation Implementations\\n\\n**client/v3/kv.go**: Defines KV interface with Put, Get, Delete, Txn operations that use the wrapped retryKVClient\\n\\n**client/v3/watch.go**: Implements Watch interface for server push notifications, handles stream resumption on connection failures with closeSendErrTimeout (250ms)\\n\\n**client/v3/lease.go**: Implements Lease interface with Grant, Revoke, KeepAlive operations and keepAliveTimeout parameter for KeepAlive stream management. The `sendKeepAliveLoop()` sends periodic keep-alive requests to maintain lease liveliness.\\n\\n## Endpoint Resolution and Management\\n\\n**client/v3/internal/resolver/resolver.go**: Implements EtcdManualResolver using gRPC's manual.Builder for endpoint state management and updates\\n\\n**client/v3/naming/resolver/resolver.go**: Provides gRPC resolver builder using etcd's endpoint manager for dynamic endpoint discovery\\n\\n**client/v3/internal/endpoint/endpoint.go**: Interprets endpoint URLs (http, https, unix, unixs) and manages credentials requirements (CredsRequire, CredsDrop, CredsOptional)\\n\\n**client/v3/naming/endpoints/endpoints.go**: Manager interface for dynamically adding/deleting/listing endpoints backed by etcd storage\\n\\n## Overall Request Flow\\n\\n1.
